## Create Model for Yandex marketplace

### Endpoint

```
POST /admin/marketplaces.json
```

### Parameters

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| marketplace\[name\]<br> required | Name |
| marketplace\[type\]<br> required | Marketplace type, e.g. Marketplace::ModelYandexMarket |
| marketplace\[shop\_name\] | Shop name |
| marketplace\[shop\_company\] | Company name |
| marketplace\[description\_type\] | 1 fo short description, 2 for full |
| marketplace\[vendor\_id\]<br> required | id of corresponding property |
| marketplace\[use\_sku\_as\_vendor\_code\] | Use sku as vendor code |
| marketplace\[pickup\] | Pickup enable |
| marketplace\[store\] | Offline store exists |
| marketplace\[delivery\_style\] | Delivery pricing type, 0 for old, 1 for new |
| marketplace\[local\_delivery\_cost\] | Local delivery cost |
| marketplace\[adult\] | 1 if products are adult-only, else 0 |
| marketplace\[utm\_label\] | UTM label |
| marketplace\[page\_encoding\]<br> required | Encoding, windows-1251 or utf-8 |
| marketplace\[image\_style\]<br> required | Image style: thumb, compact, medium, large or original |
| marketplace\[model\_type\]<br> required | Model naming type: name or sku |
| marketplace\[collection\_ids\] | Collections to load |

### Request

#### Route

```
POST /admin/marketplaces.json
```

#### Headers

```http hljs
Content-Type: application/json
Authorization: Basic ZGlnaXRhbC1nb29kczpjNTFjOTA3MDdhMTNjZTNmZmYyMTNhZmJiNWNkMTI3MA==
```

#### Body

```application/json hljs
{
  "marketplace": {
    "name": "YM",
    "type": "Marketplace::ModelYandexMarket",
    "shop_name": "eBay",
    "shop_company": "eBay",
    "description_type": 1,
    "vendor_id": 6,
    "adult": 0,
    "page_encoding": "windows-1251",
    "image_style": "oroginal",
    "collection_ids": [\
      6,\
      1,\
      2,\
      3,\
      4,\
      5,\
      8\
    ]
  }
}
```

### Response

[Simulated Response](/simulate/marketplace/create_model_for_yandex_marketplace_json)


#### Headers

```http hljs

Content-Type: application/json; charset=utf-8
```

#### Body

```application/json; charset=utf-8 hljs
{
  "id": 8,
  "name": "YM",
  "type": "Marketplace::ModelYandexMarket",
  "created_at": "2024-11-13T00:57:42.844+03:00",
  "updated_at": "2024-11-13T00:57:42.844+03:00",
  "url": "https://quentin.insales.io:3002/marketplace/8.xml",
  "collection_ids": [\
    6,\
    1,\
    2,\
    3,\
    4,\
    5,\
    8\
  ],
  "delivery_price_kind": null,
  "description_type": 1,
  "local_delivery_cost": null,
  "sales_notes": null,
  "utm_label": null,
  "vendor_id": 6,
  "page_encoding": "windows-1251",
  "shop_company": "eBay",
  "shop_name": "eBay",
  "adult": false,
  "delivery": true,
```

## Update Model for Yandex marketplace

### Endpoint

```
PUT /admin/marketplaces/:ym_marketplace_id.json
```

### Parameters

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| marketplace\[name\] | Name |
| marketplace\[shop\_name\] | Shop name |
| marketplace\[shop\_company\] | Company name |
| marketplace\[description\_type\] | 1 fo short description, 2 for full |
| marketplace\[vendor\_id\] | id of corresponding property |
| marketplace\[use\_sku\_as\_vendor\_code\] | Use sku as vendor code |
| marketplace\[pickup\] | Pickup enable |
| marketplace\[store\] | Offline store exists |
| marketplace\[delivery\_style\] | Delivery pricing type, 0 for old, 1 for new |
| marketplace\[local\_delivery\_cost\] | Local delivery cost |
| marketplace\[adult\] | 1 if products are adult-only, else 0 |
| marketplace\[utm\_label\] | UTM label |
| marketplace\[page\_encoding\] | Encoding, windows-1251 or utf-8 |
| marketplace\[image\_style\] | Image style: thumb, compact, medium, large or original |
| marketplace\[model\_type\] | Model naming type: name or sku |
| marketplace\[collection\_ids\] | Collections to load |

### Request

#### Route

```
PUT /admin/marketplaces/12.json
```

#### Headers

```http hljs
Content-Type: application/json
Authorization: Basic ZGlnaXRhbC1nb29kczpjNTFjOTA3MDdhMTNjZTNmZmYyMTNhZmJiNWNkMTI3MA==
```

```application/json hljs
      8\
    ]

}
```

# Menu

## Create menu

### Endpoint

```
POST /admin/menus.json
```

### Parameters

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| menu\[name\]<br> required | menu text |
| menu\[handle\]<br> required | handle used in liquid |

### Request

#### Route

```
POST /admin/menus.json
```

#### Headers

```http hljs
Content-Type: application/json
Authorization: Basic ZGlnaXRhbC1nb29kczpjNTFjOTA3MDdhMTNjZTNmZmYyMTNhZmJiNWNkMTI3MA==
```

#### Body

```application/json hljs
{
  "menu": {
    "name": "top menu",
    "handle": "top-menu"
  }
}
```

### Response

[Simulated Response](/simulate/menu/create_menu_json)

#### Status

```http hljs
201
```

#### Headers

```http hljs
API-Usage-Limit: 1/500
Content-Type: application/json; charset=utf-8
```

#### Body

```application/json; charset=utf-8 hljs
{
  "id": 4,
  "name": "top menu",
  "handle": "top-menu",
  "used_in_theme": false
}
```

# OAuthApp

## Create o\_auth\_app

### Endpoint

```
POST /admin/o_auth_apps.json
```

### Parameters

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| o\_auth\_app\[provider\_handle\]<br> required | provider name |
| o\_auth\_app\[client\_id\]<br> required | client id |
| o\_auth\_app\[client\_secret\]<br> required | client\_secret |
| o\_auth\_app\[issuer\]<br> required | issuer |

### Request

#### Route


# OptionName

| option\_name\[navigational\] | true by default; show in products filter on category page |

## Get option\_values for specific option

### Endpoint

```
GET /admin/option_names/:option_name_id/option_values.json
```

### Request

```

```

#### Headers

```http hljs
Authorization: Basic ZGlnaXRhbC1nb29kczpjNTFjOTA3MDdhMTNjZTNmZmYyMTNhZmJiNWNkMTI3MA==
```

## Update option\_value

### Endpoint

```

```

### Parameters

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| option\_value\[position\] | position |
| option\_value\[image\]\[filename\] | image filename, required if attachment present |
| option\_value\[image\]\[attachment\] | base64 encoded image body |
| option\_value\[image\]\[src\] | image url |

### Request

#### Route

```
PUT /admin/option_names/1/option_values/2.json
```

#### Headers

```http hljs
Content-Type: application/json
Authorization: Basic ZGlnaXRhbC1nb29kczpjNTFjOTA3MDdhMTNjZTNmZmYyMTNhZmJiNWNkMTI3MA==
```

#### Body

```application/json hljs
{
  "option_value": {
    "position": 3,
    "image": {
      "src": "https://abc.myinsales.ru/images/no_image_compact.jpg"
    }
  }
}
```

# Order

## Create discount

### Endpoint

```
PUT /admin/orders/:order_id.json
```

### Parameters

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| order\[discounts\_attributes\]<br> required | discounts attributes |
| order\[discounts\_attributes\]\[\]\[discount\]<br> required | discount amount |
| order\[discounts\_attributes\]\[\]\[type\_id\] | 1 - percent (default), 2 - money |
| order\[discounts\_attributes\]\[\]\[description\] | description text |
| order\[discounts\_attributes\]\[\]\[discount\_order\_lines\_ids\] | ids of affected order lines (all will be affected if not specified) |

### Request

#### Route

```
PUT /admin/orders/1.json
```

#### Headers

```http hljs
Content-Type: application/json
Authorization: Basic ZGlnaXRhbC1nb29kczpjNTFjOTA3MDdhMTNjZTNmZmYyMTNhZmJiNWNkMTI3MA==
```

#### Body

```application/json hljs
{
  "order": {
    "discounts_attributes": [\
      {\
        "discount": 100,\
        "type_id": 2,\
        "description": "-100 (absolute)"\

      {\
        "discount": 10,\
        "description": "10% only for first order line",\
        "discount_order_lines_ids": [\
          25\
        ]\
      }\
    ]
  }
}
```

## Create order line by product\_id

### Endpoint

```
PUT /admin/orders/:order_id.json
```

### Parameters

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| order\[order\_lines\_attributes\]<br> required | order lines attributes |
| order\[order\_lines\_attributes\]\[\]\[quantity\]<br> required | quantity |
| order\[order\_lines\_attributes\]\[\]\[vat\] | integer, VAT for order line is equal to VAT of its product, by default, products get their value from account by default,if default in account set as 'No VAT', you need to use 'force' to change VAT of order line through API; possible values depend on country, set to -1 if this product is not a subject to VAT |
| order\[order\_lines\_attributes\]\[\]\[product\_id\]<br> required | product id |

### Request

#### Route

```
PUT /admin/orders/1.json
```

#### Headers

```http hljs
Content-Type: application/json
Authorization: Basic ZGlnaXRhbC1nb29kczpjNTFjOTA3MDdhMTNjZTNmZmYyMTNhZmJiNWNkMTI3MA==
```

#### Body

```application/json hljs
{
  "order": {
    "order_lines_attributes": [\
      {\
        "product_id": 1,\
        "quantity": 1,\
        "vat": 18\
      }\
    ]
  }
}
```

### Response

[Simulated Response](/simulate/order/create_order_line_by_product_id_json)

#### Status

```http hljs
200
```

#### Headers

```http hljs
API-Usage-Limit: 1/500
Content-Type: application/json; charset=utf-8
```

#### Body

```application/json; charset=utf-8 hljs
{
  "fields_values": [\
    {\
      "id": 91,\

      "updated_at": "2024-11-13T00:57:08.137+03:00",\
      "type": "Текст",\
      "name": "special",\
      "handle": "my_awesome_field"\
    }\
  ],
  "order_lines": [\
    {\
      "id": 24,\
      "order_id": 1,\
```

## Create order line by variant\_id

### Endpoint

```
PUT /admin/orders/:order_id.json
```

### Parameters

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| order\[order\_lines\_attributes\]<br> required | order lines attributes |
| order\[order\_lines\_attributes\]\[\]\[quantity\]<br> required | quantity |
| order\[order\_lines\_attributes\]\[\]\[vat\] | integer, VAT for order line is equal to VAT of its product, by default, products get their value from account by default,if default in account set as 'No VAT', you need to use 'force' to change VAT of order line through API; possible values depend on country, set to -1 if this product is not a subject to VAT |
| order\[order\_lines\_attributes\]\[\]\[variant\_id\]<br> required | variant id |

### Request

#### Route

```
PUT /admin/orders/1.json
```

#### Headers

```http hljs
Content-Type: application/json
Authorization: Basic ZGlnaXRhbC1nb29kczpjNTFjOTA3MDdhMTNjZTNmZmYyMTNhZmJiNWNkMTI3MA==
```

#### Body

```application/json hljs
{
  "order": {
    "order_lines_attributes": [\
      {\
        "variant_id": 1,\
        "quantity": 1,\
        "vat": -1\
      }\
    ]
  }
}
```

### Response

[Simulated Response](/simulate/order/create_order_line_by_variant_id_json)

#### Status

```http hljs
200
```

#### Headers

```http hljs
API-Usage-Limit: 1/500
Content-Type: application/json; charset=utf-8
```

## Create order with bundle

### Endpoint

```
POST /admin/orders.json
```

### Parameters

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| order\[order\_lines\_attributes\]<br> required | order lines attributes |
| order\[order\_lines\_attributes\]\[\]\[quantity\]<br> required | quantity |
| order\[order\_lines\_attributes\]\[\]\[variant\_id\]<br> required | variant id |
| order\[order\_lines\_attributes\]\[\]\[vat\] | do not set vat for bundle, because after order creation bundle will break into bundle components, which have their own VAT rates |
| order\[client\]<br> required | client info |
| order\[client\]\[name\] | client name |
| order\[client\]\[email\] | client email |
| order\[client\]\[phone\]<br> required | client phone |
| order\[client\]\[consent\_to\_personal\_data\]<br> required | consent to personal data |
| order\[shipping\_address\_attributes\]<br> required | array of shipping address attributes |
| order\[shipping\_address\_attributes\]\[address\] | shipping address |
| order\[shipping\_address\_attributes\]\[full\_locality\_name\]<br> required | full locality name |
| order\[delivery\_variant\_id\]<br> required | delivery variant id |
| order\[payment\_gateway\_id\]<br> required | payment gateway id |
| order\[coupon\] | discount code |

### Request

#### Route

```
POST /admin/orders.json
```

#### Headers

```http hljs
Content-Type: application/json
Authorization: Basic ZGlnaXRhbC1nb29kczpjNTFjOTA3MDdhMTNjZTNmZmYyMTNhZmJiNWNkMTI3MA==
```

#### Body

```application/json hljs
{
  "order": {
    "order_lines_attributes": [\
      {\
        "variant_id": 5,\
        "quantity": 2\
      }\
    ],
    "client": {
      "name": "Vasya",
      "email": "vasya@example.com",
      "phone": "79111112233",
      "consent_to_personal_data": true
    },
    "shipping_address_attributes": {
      "address": "Moscow, Krasnaya Presna 24",
      "full_locality_name": "Moscow"
    },
    "delivery_variant_id": 1,
    "payment_gateway_id": 1,
    "coupon": "20% discount"
  }
}
```

### Response

[Simulated Response](/simulate/order/create_order_with_bundle_json)

#### Status

```http hljs
201
```


## Create order with product

### Endpoint

```
POST /admin/orders.json
```

### Parameters

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| order\[order\_lines\_attributes\]<br> required | order lines attributes |
| order\[order\_lines\_attributes\]\[\]\[quantity\]<br> required | quantity |
| order\[order\_lines\_attributes\]\[\]\[variant\_id\]<br> required | variant id |
| order\[order\_lines\_attributes\]\[\]\[vat\] | integer, VAT for order line is equal to VAT of its product, by default, products get their value from account by default,if default in account set as 'No VAT', you need to use 'force' to change VAT of order line through API; possible values depend on country, set to -1 if this product is not a subject to VAT |
| order\[client\]<br> required | client info |
| order\[client\]\[name\] | client name |
| order\[client\]\[email\] | client email |
| order\[client\]\[phone\]<br> required | client phone |
| order\[shipping\_address\_attributes\]<br> required | array of shipping address attributes |
| order\[shipping\_address\_attributes\]\[address\] | shipping address |
| order\[delivery\_variant\_id\]<br> required | delivery variant id |
| order\[payment\_gateway\_id\]<br> required | payment gateway id |
| order\[coupon\] | discount code |

### Request

#### Route

```
POST /admin/orders.json
```

#### Headers

```http hljs
Content-Type: application/json
Authorization: Basic ZGlnaXRhbC1nb29kczpjNTFjOTA3MDdhMTNjZTNmZmYyMTNhZmJiNWNkMTI3MA==
```

#### Body

```application/json hljs
{
  "order": {
    "order_lines_attributes": [\
      {\
        "variant_id": 3,\
        "quantity": 2,\
        "vat": 10\
      }\
    ],
    "client": {
      "name": "Vasya",
      "email": "vasya@example.com",
      "phone": "79111112233"
    },
    "shipping_address_attributes": {
      "address": "Moscow, Krasnaya Presna 24"
    },
    "delivery_variant_id": 1,
    "payment_gateway_id": 1,
    "coupon": "20% discount"
  }
}
```

## Get order

### Endpoint

```
GET /admin/orders/:order_id.json
```

### Request

#### Route

```
GET /admin/orders/1.json
```

#### Headers

```http hljs
Authorization: Basic ZGlnaXRhbC1nb29kczpjNTFjOTA3MDdhMTNjZTNmZmYyMTNhZmJiNWNkMTI3MA==
```

### Response

[Simulated Response](/simulate/order/get_order_json)

```http hljs
200
```

```http hljs
API-Usage-Limit: 1/500
Content-Type: application/json; charset=utf-8
```

## Get orders count

### Endpoint

```
GET /admin/orders/count.json
```

### Parameters

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| fulfillment\_status | array of statuses |
| delivery\_variant | array of delivery variant ids |
| payment\_gateway\_id | array of payment gateway ids |

### Request

#### Route

```
GET /admin/orders/count.json
```

#### Headers

```http hljs
Authorization: Basic ZGlnaXRhbC1nb29kczpjNTFjOTA3MDdhMTNjZTNmZmYyMTNhZmJiNWNkMTI3MA==
```

### Response

[Simulated Response](/simulate/order/get_orders_count_json)

#### Status

```http hljs
200
```

#### Headers

```http hljs
API-Usage-Limit: 1/500
Content-Type: application/json; charset=utf-8
```

#### Body

```application/json; charset=utf-8 hljs
{
  "count": 6
}
```

## Get orders

### Endpoint

```
GET /admin/orders.json
```

### Parameters

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| fulfillment\_status | array of statuses |
| delivery\_variant | array of delivery variant ids |
| payment\_gateway\_id | array of payment gateway ids |
| updated\_since | Set datetime to get only data updated after it. |
| from\_id | Set id to get only data starting from it. |
| per\_page | Quantity of objects per page. |

### Request

#### Route

```
GET /admin/orders.json?fulfillment_status[]=new&fulfillment_status[]=delivered&delivery_variant[]=1&delivery_variant[]=2&payment_gateway_id[]=1&payment_gateway_id[]=3
```

#### Headers


## Remove discount

### Endpoint

```
PUT /admin/orders/:order_id.json
```

### Parameters

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| order\[discounts\_attributes\]<br> required | discounts attributes |
| order\[discounts\_attributes\]\[\]\[id\]<br> required | discount id |
| order\[discounts\_attributes\]\[\]\[\_destroy\]<br> required | destroy marker (1 or true) |

### Request

#### Route

```
PUT /admin/orders/1.json
```

#### Headers

```http hljs
Content-Type: application/json
Authorization: Basic ZGlnaXRhbC1nb29kczpjNTFjOTA3MDdhMTNjZTNmZmYyMTNhZmJiNWNkMTI3MA==
```

#### Body

```application/json hljs
{
  "order": {
    "discounts_attributes": [\
      {\
        "id": 17,\
        "_destroy": true\
      }\
    ]
  }
}
```

[Simulated Response](/simulate/order/remove_discount_json)

#### Status

```http hljs
200
```

#### Headers

```http hljs
API-Usage-Limit: 1/500
Content-Type: application/json; charset=utf-8
```

## Remove order line

### Endpoint

```
PUT /admin/orders/:order_id.json
```

### Parameters

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| order\[order\_lines\_attributes\]<br> required | order lines attributes |
| order\[order\_lines\_attributes\]\[\]\[id\]<br> required | order line id |
| order\[order\_lines\_attributes\]\[\]\[\_destroy\]<br> required | destroy marker (1 or true) |

#### Route


```http hljs
Content-Type: application/json
```

## Update custom status

This query updates custom status. Despite the fact that “order\[fulfillment\_status\]” parameter is permitted, using both of the parameters is strongly discouraged. Please, keep in mind that if both parameters are transfered they MUST be compatible. Please, notice that you CAN’T update custom status using order\[custom\_status\]\[permalink\] parameter.

### Endpoint

```
PUT /admin/orders/:order_id.json
```

### Parameters

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| order\[custom\_status\_permalink\]<br> required | custom status |
| order\[fulfillment\_status\] | fulfillment status |

### Request

#### Route

```
PUT /admin/orders/1.json
```

#### Headers

```http hljs
Content-Type: application/json
Authorization: Basic ZGlnaXRhbC1nb29kczpjNTFjOTA3MDdhMTNjZTNmZmYyMTNhZmJiNWNkMTI3MA==
```

#### Body

```application/json hljs
{
  "order": {
    "custom_status_permalink": "v-obrabotke"
  }
}
```

### Response

[Simulated Response](/simulate/order/update_custom_status_json)

#### Status

```http hljs
200
```

#### Headers

```http hljs
API-Usage-Limit: 1/500
Content-Type: application/json; charset=utf-8
```

## Update discount

### Endpoint

```
PUT /admin/orders/:order_id.json
```

### Parameters

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| order\[discounts\_attributes\]<br> required | discounts attributes |
| order\[discounts\_attributes\]\[\]\[id\]<br> required | discount id |
| order\[discounts\_attributes\]\[\]\[discount\] | discount amount |
| order\[discounts\_attributes\]\[\]\[type\_id\] | 1 - percent (default), 2 - money |
| order\[discounts\_attributes\]\[\]\[description\] | description text |
| order\[discounts\_attributes\]\[\]\[discount\_order\_lines\_ids\] | ids of affected order lines (all will be affected if not specified) |

### Request

#### Route

```
PUT /admin/orders/1.json
```

#### Headers

```http hljs
Content-Type: application/json
Authorization: Basic ZGlnaXRhbC1nb29kczpjNTFjOTA3MDdhMTNjZTNmZmYyMTNhZmJiNWNkMTI3MA==
```

#### Body

```application/json hljs
{
  "order": {
    "discounts_attributes": {
      "1": {
        "id": 19,
        "discount_order_lines_ids": [\
          31\
        ]
      }
    }
  }
}
```

### Response

[Simulated Response](/simulate/order/update_discount_json)

```http hljs
200
```

```http hljs
API-Usage-Limit: 1/500
Content-Type: application/json; charset=utf-8
```

## Update order

### Endpoint

```
PUT /admin/orders/:order_id.json
```

### Parameters

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| order\[client\_attributes\] | client info |
| order\[client\_attributes\]\[name\] | client name |
| order\[client\_attributes\]\[email\] | client email |
| order\[client\_attributes\]\[phone\] | client phone |
| order\[delivery\_variant\_id\] | delivery variant id |
| order\[payment\_gateway\_id\] | payment gateway id |
| order\[coupon\] | discount code |
| order\[comment\] | client comment to order |
| order\[manager\_comment\] | manager comment to order |
| order\[financial\_status\] | pending or paid |
| order\[fields\_values\_attributes\] | fields values array |
| order\[shipping\_address\_attributes\] | array of shipping address attributes |
| order\[discounts\_attributes\] | array of discounts attributes |
| order\[warehouse\_id\] | id of a warehouse to reserve products on |

### Request

#### Route

```
PUT /admin/orders/1.json
```

#### Headers

```http hljs
Content-Type: application/json
Authorization: Basic ZGlnaXRhbC1nb29kczpjNTFjOTA3MDdhMTNjZTNmZmYyMTNhZmJiNWNkMTI3MA==
```

#### Body

```application/json hljs
{
  "order": {
    "client_attributes": {
      "id": 2,
      "name": "Ivan",
      "email": "ivan@example.com",
      "phone": "79111113344",
      "fields_values_attributes": [\
        {\
          "field_id": 255,\
          "value": "new!"\
        }\
      ]
    },
    "delivery_variant_id": 3,
    "payment_gateway_id": 4,
    "coupon": "20% discount",
    "comment": "Please call from 9 to 18",
    "manager_comment": "New client",
    "financial_status": "paid",
    "fields_values_attributes": [\
      {\
        "handle": "my_awesome_field",\
        "value": "new value"\
      }\
    ],
    "shipping_address_attributes": {
      "fields_values_attributes": [\
        {\
          "field_id": 256,\
          "value": "new value!"\
        }\
      ]
    },
    "warehouse_id": 42
  }
}
```

[Simulated Response](/simulate/order/update_order_json)

```http hljs
200
```



## Update order line

### Endpoint

```
PUT /admin/orders/:order_id.json
```

### Parameters

| Name | Description | Type |
| --- | --- | --- |
| order\[order\_lines\_attributes\]<br> required | order lines attributes |  |
| order\[order\_lines\_attributes\]\[\]\[id\]<br> required | order line id |  |
| order\[order\_lines\_attributes\]\[\]\[sale\_price\] | order line sale price |  |
| order\[order\_lines\_attributes\]\[\]\[quantity\] | order line quantity |  |
| order\[order\_lines\_attributes\]\[\]\[comment\] | order line comment |  |
| order\[order\_lines\_attributes\]\[\]\[vat\] | integer, VAT for order line is equal to VAT of its product, by default, products get their value from account by default,if default in account set as 'No VAT', you need to use 'force' to change VAT of order line through API; possible values depend on country, set to -1 if this product is not a subject to VAT |  |
| order\[order\_lines\_attributes\]\[\]\[marking\_codes\] | array of marking codes | array |

### Request

#### Route

```
PUT /admin/orders/1.json
```

#### Headers

```http hljs
Content-Type: application/json
Authorization: Basic ZGlnaXRhbC1nb29kczpjNTFjOTA3MDdhMTNjZTNmZmYyMTNhZmJiNWNkMTI3MA==
```

#### Body

```application/json hljs
{
  "order": {
    "order_lines_attributes": [\
      {\
        "id": 1,\
        "sale_price": 100,\
        "quantity": 2,\
        "comment": "New comment",\
        "vat": 0,\
        "marking_codes": [\
          "2605f502ffe3804cd0e2",\
          "6ce8c8c2d13638b63851"\
        ]\
      }\
    ]
  }
}
```

### Response

[Simulated Response](/simulate/order/update_order_line_json)

#### Status

```http hljs
200
```

#### Headers

```http hljs
API-Usage-Limit: 1/500
Content-Type: application/json; charset=utf-8
```

## Update shipping address

### Endpoint

```
PUT /admin/orders/:order_id.json
```

### Parameters

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| order\[shipping\_address\_attributes\]<br> required | array of shipping address attributes |
| order\[shipping\_address\_attributes\]\[address\]<br> required | shipping address |

### Request

#### Route

```
PUT /admin/orders/1.json
```

#### Headers

```http hljs
Content-Type: application/json
Authorization: Basic ZGlnaXRhbC1nb29kczpjNTFjOTA3MDdhMTNjZTNmZmYyMTNhZmJiNWNkMTI3MA==
```

#### Body

```application/json hljs
{
  "order": {
    "shipping_address_attributes": {
      "address": "Moscow, Znamenka 12"
    }
  }
}
```

```http hljs
200
```

# Outlet

## Create outlet

### Endpoint

```
POST /admin/outlets.json
```

### Parameters

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| outlet\[title\]<br> required | title |
| outlet\[description\] | description |
| outlet\[address\]<br> required | address in text way |
| outlet\[price\]<br> required | delivery price |
| outlet\[latitude\]<br> required | point latitude |
| outlet\[longitude\]<br> required | point longitude |

### Request

#### Route

```
POST /admin/outlets.json
```

#### Headers

```http hljs
Content-Type: application/json
Authorization: Basic ZGlnaXRhbC1nb29kczpjNTFjOTA3MDdhMTNjZTNmZmYyMTNhZmJiNWNkMTI3MA==
```

#### Body

```application/json hljs
{
  "outlet": {
    "title": "Point 2",
    "description": "Point description",
    "address": "some address",
    "price": 300,
    "latitude": 55.7558,
    "longitude": 37.6173
  }
}
```

### Response

[Simulated Response](/simulate/outlet/create_outlet_json)

#### Status

```http hljs
201
```

#### Headers

```http hljs
API-Usage-Limit: 1/500
Content-Type: application/json; charset=utf-8
```

#### Body

```application/json; charset=utf-8 hljs
{
  "id": 8,
  "account_id": 1,
  "delivery_variant_id": 35,
  "price": "300.0",
  "title_translations": [\
    "Point 2"\
  ],
  "description_translations": [\
    "Point description"\
  ],
  "address": "some address",
  "latitude": "55.7558",
  "longitude": "37.6173",
  "created_at": "2024-11-13T00:56:52.387+03:00",
  "updated_at": "2024-11-13T00:56:52.387+03:00",
  "title": "Point 2",
  "description": "Point description"
}
```

## Update outlet

### Endpoint

```
PUT /admin/outlets/:outlet_id.json
```

### Parameters

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| outlet\[title\]<br> required | title |
| outlet\[description\] | description |
| outlet\[address\]<br> required | address in text way |
| outlet\[price\]<br> required | delivery price |
| outlet\[latitude\]<br> required | point latitude |
| outlet\[longitude\]<br> required | point longitude |

### Request

#### Route

```
PUT /admin/outlets/10.json
```

#### Headers

```http hljs
Content-Type: application/json
```

# Page

## Create page

### Endpoint

```
POST /admin/pages.json
```

### Parameters

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| page\[title\]<br> required | page title |
| page\[content\]<br> required | page content |
| page\[permalink\] | permalink on /page/\* |
| page\[html\_title\] | html title tag content |
| page\[meta\_keywords\] | html meta words on page |
| page\[meta\_description\] | html meta description |
| page\[created\_at\] | publication date |

### Request

#### Route

```
POST /admin/pages.json
```

#### Headers

```http hljs
Content-Type: application/json
Authorization: Basic ZGlnaXRhbC1nb29kczpjNTFjOTA3MDdhMTNjZTNmZmYyMTNhZmJiNWNkMTI3MA==
```

#### Body

```application/json hljs
{
  "page": {
    "title": "new page",
    "content": "<p>content of my page<p>",
    "permalink": "first_page",
    "html_title": "HTML TAG TITLE",
    "meta_keywords": "new cool products",
    "meta_description": "It's a page about our new products",
    "created_at": "2014-09-09"
  }
}
```

### Response

[Simulated Response](/simulate/page/create_page_json)

#### Status

```http hljs
201
```

#### Headers

```http hljs
API-Usage-Limit: 1/500
Content-Type: application/json; charset=utf-8
```

#### Body

```application/json; charset=utf-8 hljs
{
  "id": 20,
  "title": "new page",
  "content": "<p>content of my page<p>",
  "permalink": "first_page",
  "is_main": false,
  "html_title": "HTML TAG TITLE",
  "meta_keywords": "new cool products",
  "meta_description": "It's a page about our new products",
  "created_at": "2014-09-09T00:00:00.000+04:00",
  "updated_at": "2024-11-13T00:57:52.000+03:00",
  "custom_template": null
}
```

# PaymentGateway

## Create Cod or Custom payment\_gateway

### Endpoint

```
POST /admin/payment_gateways.json
```

### Parameters

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| payment\_gateway\[title\]<br> required | title |
| payment\_gateway\[margin\] | margin measured in percentage and applied to order price with current payment method; it should fall in the range from -100 to 1000 |
| payment\_gateway\[position\] | position in payment gateways list |
| payment\_gateway\[type\]<br> required | available types: PaymentGateway::Cod, PaymentGateway::Custom |
| payment\_gateway\[description\] | description |
| payment\_gateway\[payment\_delivery\_variants\_attributes\] | array of available delivery variants for this payment gateway; payment gateway is unavailable if list is empty |
| payment\_gateway\[payment\_delivery\_variants\_attributes\]\[delivery\_variant\_id\] | id of delivery variant |
| payment\_gateway\[add\_delivery\_variants\] | set all delivery variants available for this payment gateway |

### Request

#### Route

```
POST /admin/payment_gateways.json
```

#### Headers

```http hljs
Content-Type: application/json
Authorization: Basic ZGlnaXRhbC1nb29kczpjNTFjOTA3MDdhMTNjZTNmZmYyMTNhZmJiNWNkMTI3MA==
```

#### Body

```application/json hljs
{
  "payment_gateway": {
    "title": "cash on delivery",
    "margin": 10,
    "type": "PaymentGateway::Cod",
    "description": "text",
    "payment_delivery_variants_attributes": [\
      {\
        "delivery_variant_id": 1\
      }\
    ]
  }
}
```

### Response

[Simulated Response](/simulate/paymentgateway/create_cod_or_custom_payment_gateway_json)

#### Status

```http hljs
201
```

#### Headers

```http hljs
API-Usage-Limit: 1/500
Content-Type: application/json; charset=utf-8
```

#### Body

```application/json; charset=utf-8 hljs
{
  "id": 35,
  "position": 4,
  "type": "PaymentGateway::Cod",
  "created_at": "2024-11-13T00:56:53.000+03:00",
  "updated_at": "2024-11-13T00:56:53.000+03:00",
  "margin": "10.0",
  "available_for_individual_clients": true,
  "available_for_juridical_clients": true,
  "title": "cash on delivery",
  "description": "text",
  "payment_delivery_variants": [\
    {\
      "id": 58,\
      "delivery_variant_id": 1,\
      "created_at": "2024-11-13T00:56:53.000+03:00"\
    }\
  ]
}
```

## Create External payment\_gateway

### Endpoint

```
POST /admin/payment_gateways.json
```

### Parameters

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| payment\_gateway\[title\]<br> required | title |
| payment\_gateway\[margin\] | margin measured in percentage and added to order price with current payment method; it should fall in the range from -100 to 1000 |
| payment\_gateway\[position\] | position in payment gateways list |
| payment\_gateway\[type\]<br> required | PaymentGateway::External |
| payment\_gateway\[description\] | description |
| payment\_gateway\[payment\_delivery\_variants\_attributes\] | array of available delivery variants for this payment gateway; payment gateway is unavailable if list is empty |
| payment\_gateway\[payment\_delivery\_variants\_attributes\]\[delivery\_variant\_id\] | id of delivery variant |
| payment\_gateway\[url\]<br> required | url of external payment gateway |
| payment\_gateway\[shop\_id\]<br> required | shop id - store identificator for external systems |
| payment\_gateway\[send\_order\] | set true to send order\_lines information to the "url"; parameter name - "order\_json"; do not forget add "order\_json" to signature validation to the end of the string. |
| payment\_gateway\[add\_delivery\_variants\] | set all delivery variants available for this payment gateway |
| payment\_gateway\[redirect\_to\_payment\] | true by default; if true automatically redirect to payment after successful order creation; |
| payment\_gateway\[convert\_currency\] | iso code, if you would like to convert order amount from site currency to another currency |

### Request

#### Route

```
POST /admin/payment_gateways.json
```

#### Headers

```http hljs
Content-Type: application/json
Authorization: Basic ZGlnaXRhbC1nb29kczpjNTFjOTA3MDdhMTNjZTNmZmYyMTNhZmJiNWNkMTI3MA==
```

#### Body

```application/json hljs
{
  "payment_gateway": {
    "title": "external payment gateway",
    "margin": 10,
    "type": "PaymentGateway::External",
    "description": "text",
    "payment_delivery_variants_attributes": [\
      {\
        "delivery_variant_id": 1\
      }\
    ],
    "url": "payment-gateway.ru/transactions/create",
    "shop_id": "123",
    "redirect_to_payment": false,
    "convert_currency": "LVL"
  }
}
```

### Response

[Simulated Response](/simulate/paymentgateway/create_external_payment_gateway_json)

#### Status

```http hljs
201
```

#### Headers

```http hljs
API-Usage-Limit: 1/500
Content-Type: application/json; charset=utf-8
```

#### Body

```application/json; charset=utf-8 hljs
{
  "id": 37,
  "position": 4,
  "type": "PaymentGateway::External",
  "created_at": "2024-11-13T00:56:53.000+03:00",
  "updated_at": "2024-11-13T00:56:53.000+03:00",
  "margin": "10.0",
  "available_for_individual_clients": true,
  "available_for_juridical_clients": true,
  "title": "external payment gateway",
  "description": "text",
  "password": "f5d9fba6c71cb039",
  "url": "payment-gateway.ru/transactions/create",
  "shop_id": "123",
  "send_order": null,
  "convert_currency": "LVL",
  "widget_mode": null,
  "window_mode": null,
  "widget_html_code": null,
  "success_url": "http://quentin.insales.io:3002/payments/external/37/success",
  "fail_url": "http://quentin.insales.io:3002/payments/external/37/fail",
  "server_url": "http://quentin.insales.io:3002/payments/external/37/server",
  "redirect_to_payment": false,
  "payment_delivery_variants": [\
    {\
      "id": 60,\
      "delivery_variant_id": 1,\
      "created_at": "2024-11-13T00:56:53.000+03:00"\
    }\
  ]
}
```

## Update payment\_gateway

### Endpoint

```
PUT /admin/payment_gateways/:payment_gateway_id_1.json
```

### Parameters

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| payment\_gateway\[title\] | title |
| payment\_gateway\[margin\] | margin measured in percentage and added to order price with current payment method; it should fall in the range from -100 to 1000 |
| payment\_gateway\[position\] | position in payment gateways list |
| payment\_gateway\[description\] | description |
| payment\_gateway\[payment\_delivery\_variants\_attributes\] | array of available delivery variants for this payment gateway. payment gateway is unavailable if list is empty |
| payment\_gateway\[payment\_delivery\_variants\_attributes\]\[\_destroy\] | set it 1 to delete delivery variant for this payment gateway |
| delivery\_variant\[payment\_delivery\_variants\_attributes\]\[id\] | only for removal: specify id of payment gateway and delivery variant binding you want to delete |
| delivery\_variant\[payment\_delivery\_variants\_attributes\]\[delivery\_variant\_id\] | for creation: specify id of delivery variant you want to bind with this payment gateway |

### Request

#### Route

```
PUT /admin/payment_gateways/1.json
```

#### Headers

```http hljs
Content-Type: application/json
Authorization: Basic ZGlnaXRhbC1nb29kczpjNTFjOTA3MDdhMTNjZTNmZmYyMTNhZmJiNWNkMTI3MA==
```

#### Body

```application/json hljs
{
  "payment_gateway": {
    "title": "cash",
    "margin": 10,
    "description": "description",
    "payment_delivery_variants_attributes": [\
      {\
        "_destroy": 1,\
        "id": 2\
      },\
      {\
        "delivery_variant_id": 2\
      }\
    ]
  }
}
```

### Response

[Simulated Response](/simulate/paymentgateway/update_payment_gateway_json)

#### Status

```http hljs
200
```

#### Headers

```http hljs
API-Usage-Limit: 1/500
Content-Type: application/json; charset=utf-8
```

#### Body

```application/json; charset=utf-8 hljs
{
  "margin": "10.0",
  "id": 1,
  "position": 1,
  "type": "PaymentGateway::Cod",
  "created_at": "2009-03-30T04:37:32.000+04:00",
  "updated_at": "2024-11-13T00:56:53.000+03:00",
  "available_for_individual_clients": true,
  "available_for_juridical_clients": true,
  "title": "cash",
  "description": "description",
  "payment_delivery_variants": [\
    {\
      "id": 1,\
      "delivery_variant_id": 1,\
      "created_at": "2024-11-13T00:56:24.000+03:00"\
    },\
    {\
      "id": 2,\
      "delivery_variant_id": 2,\
      "created_at": "2024-11-13T00:56:24.000+03:00"\
    }\
  ]
}
```

# Product

## Create bundle

### Endpoint

```
POST /admin/products.json
```

### Parameters

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| product\[category\_id\]<br> required | category id |
| product\[title\]<br> required | title |
| product\[description\] | description |
| product\[short\_description\] | short description |
| product\[sort\_weight\] | sort weight |
| product\[bundle\]<br> required | bundle |
| product\[variants\_attributes\]<br> required | variants attributes |
| product\[vat\] | do not set VAT for bundle because order lines will be created with its components, which have their own VAT |
| product\[product\_bundle\_components\_attributes\]<br> required | product bundle components attributes |

### Request

#### Route

```
POST /admin/products.json
```

#### Headers

```http hljs
Content-Type: application/json
Authorization: Basic ZGlnaXRhbC1nb29kczpjNTFjOTA3MDdhMTNjZTNmZmYyMTNhZmJiNWNkMTI3MA==
```

#### Body

```application/json hljs
{
  "product": {
    "category_id": 1,
    "title": "Van Gogh Ruled Peach Notebook",
    "bundle": true,
    "variants_attributes": [\
      {\
        "price": 100\
      }\
    ],
    "product_bundle_components_attributes": [\
      {\
        "variant_id": 1,\
        "quantity": 2,\
        "free": false\
      }\
    ]
  }
}
```

[Simulated Response](/simulate/product/create_bundle_json)

```http hljs
201
```

```http hljs
API-Usage-Limit: 1/500
```

## Create product

### Endpoint

```
POST /admin/products.json
```

### Parameters

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| product\[category\_id\]<br> required | category id |
| product\[title\]<br> required | title |
| product\[description\] | description |
| product\[short\_description\] | short description |
| product\[variants\_attributes\]<br> required | variants attributes |
| product\[sort\_weight\] | sort weight |
| product\[ignore\_discounts\] | set to 1 to make this product ignore discounts |
| product\[vat\] | integer, default value is set in account settings, if default in account set as 'No VAT' you cannot change VAT of products through API; possible values depend on country, set to -1 if this product is not a subject to VAT |
| product\[product\_field\_values\_attributes\] | product field values attributes |

### Request

#### Route

```
POST /admin/products.json
```

#### Headers

```http hljs
Content-Type: application/json
Authorization: Basic ZGlnaXRhbC1nb29kczpjNTFjOTA3MDdhMTNjZTNmZmYyMTNhZmJiNWNkMTI3MA==
```

#### Body

```application/json hljs
{
  "product": {
    "category_id": 1,
    "title": "Van Gogh Ruled Peach Notebook",
    "variants_attributes": [\
      {\
        "sku": "QP021MVEN-r",\
        "quantity": 1,\
        "price": 740\
      }\
    ],
    "ignore_discounts": 1,
    "vat": -1,
    "product_field_values_attributes": [\
      {\
        "handle": "handle",\
        "value": 12345\
      }\
    ]
  }
}
```

[Simulated Response](/simulate/product/create_product_json)


## Get products

### Endpoint

```
GET /admin/products.json
```

### Parameters

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| updated\_since | Set datetime to get only data updated after it. |
| from\_id | Set id to get only data starting from it. |
| per\_page | Quantity of objects per page. |
| with\_deleted | Set to true to get also deleted products. |
| deleted | Set to true to get only deleted products. |
| variant\_fields | List of required fields separated with \`,\`. Possible values are: id,title,product\_id,sku,barcode,dimensions,available. |

### Request

#### Route

```
GET /admin/products.json?updated_since=2009-01-04+14%3A44%3A43+%2B0300
```

#### Headers

```http hljs
Authorization: Basic ZGlnaXRhbC1nb29kczpjNTFjOTA3MDdhMTNjZTNmZmYyMTNhZmJiNWNkMTI3MA==
```

#### Query Parameters

```
updated_since=2009-01-04 14:44:43 +0300
```

[Simulated Response](/simulate/product/get_products_json)

## Update bundle

### Endpoint

```
PUT /admin/products/4.json
```

### Parameters

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| product\[title\] | title |
| product\[ignore\_discounts\] | set to 1 to make this product ignore discounts |
| product\[vat\] | do not set VAT for bundle because order lines will be created with its components, which have their own VAT |
| product\[product\_bundle\_components\_attributes\] | component without the specified identifier (id) will be created (variant\_id is required);<br>component with id will be updated (variant\_id is optional);<br>component with id and (\_destroy: true) attribute will be destroyed; |

### Request

#### Route

```
PUT /admin/products/4.json
```

#### Headers

```http hljs
Content-Type: application/json
Authorization: Basic ZGlnaXRhbC1nb29kczpjNTFjOTA3MDdhMTNjZTNmZmYyMTNhZmJiNWNkMTI3MA==
```

#### Body

```application/json hljs
{
  "product": {
    "product_bundle_components_attributes": [\
      {\
        "variant_id": 3,\
        "quantity": 2,\
        "free": false\
      },\
      {\
        "id": 1,\
        "quantity": 4\
      },\
      {\
        "id": 2,\
        "_destroy": true\
      }\
    ]
  }
}
```

### Response

[Simulated Response](/simulate/product/update_bundle_json)

#### Status

```http hljs
200
```

#### Headers

```http hljs
API-Usage-Limit: 1/500
Content-Type: application/json; charset=utf-8
```

#### Body


## Update product

### Endpoint

```
PUT /admin/products/:product_id.json
```

### Parameters

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| product\[title\] | title |
| product\[ignore\_discounts\] | set to 1 to make this product ignore discounts |
| product\[vat\] | integer, default value is set in account settings, if default in account set as 'No VAT' you cannot change VAT of products through API; possible values depend on country, set to -1 if this product is not a subject to VAT |
| product\[product\_field\_values\_attributes\] | product field values attributes |

### Request

#### Route

```
PUT /admin/products/1.json
```

#### Headers

```http hljs
Content-Type: application/json
Authorization: Basic ZGlnaXRhbC1nb29kczpjNTFjOTA3MDdhMTNjZTNmZmYyMTNhZmJiNWNkMTI3MA==
```

#### Body

```application/json hljs
{
  "product": {
    "title": "Van Gogh Notebook",
    "ignore_discounts": 1,
    "vat": 10,
    "product_field_values_attributes": [\
      {\
        "handle": "handle",\
        "value": 12345\
      }\
    ]
  }
}
```

### Response

[Simulated Response](/simulate/product/update_product_json)

#### Status

```http hljs
200
```

#### Headers

```http hljs
API-Usage-Limit: 1/500
Content-Type: application/json; charset=utf-8
```

```application/json; charset=utf-8 hljs
          "id": 1,\
          "variant_field_id": 1,\
          "value": "some variant field value"\
        }\
      ],\
      "option_values": [\
        {\
          "id": 1,\
          "option_name_id": 1,\
          "position": 1,\
          "title": "Red",\
          "image_url": null\
        }\
      ]\
    }\
  ],
  "product_bundle_components": [\
\
  ]
}
```

# ProductField

## Create product\_field

### Endpoint

```
POST /admin/product_fields.json
```

### Parameters

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| product\_field\[title\]<br> required | title |
| product\_field\[handle\]<br> required | handle used in liquid |
| product\_field\[type\]<br> required | ProductField::TextArea - textarea, ProductField::TextField - textfield |
| product\_field\[position\] | position in product\_fields list |
| product\_field\[is\_hidden\] | boolean |
| product\_field\[is\_indexed\] | boolean |

### Request

#### Route

```
POST /admin/product_fields.json
```

#### Headers

```http hljs
Content-Type: application/json
Authorization: Basic ZGlnaXRhbC1nb29kczpjNTFjOTA3MDdhMTNjZTNmZmYyMTNhZmJiNWNkMTI3MA==
```

#### Body

```application/json hljs
{
  "product_field": {
    "title": "Size",
    "handle": "size",
    "type": "ProductField::TextArea"
  }
}
```

### Response

[Simulated Response](/simulate/productfield/create_product_field_json)

#### Status

```http hljs
201
```

#### Headers

```http hljs
API-Usage-Limit: 1/500
Content-Type: application/json; charset=utf-8
```

#### Body

```application/json; charset=utf-8 hljs
{
  "id": 8,
  "handle": "size",
  "type": "ProductField::TextArea",
  "application_id": 1,
  "position": 3,
  "is_hidden": null,
  "is_indexed": null,
  "title": "Size",
  "application_title": "Цифровые товары"
}
```

# Property

## Create property

### Endpoint

```
POST /admin/properties.json
```

### Parameters

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| property\[title\]<br> required | title |
| property\[permalink\] | permalink |
| property\[position\] | position in property list |
| property\[backoffice\] | show in backoffice |
| property\[is\_hidden\] | hide in product page on site |
| property\[is\_navigational\] | show in products filter on category page |

### Request

#### Route

```
POST /admin/properties.json
```

#### Headers

```http hljs
Content-Type: application/json
Authorization: Basic ZGlnaXRhbC1nb29kczpjNTFjOTA3MDdhMTNjZTNmZmYyMTNhZmJiNWNkMTI3MA==
```

#### Body

```application/json hljs
{
  "property": {
    "title": "Country",
    "permalink": "country",
    "backoffice": true,
    "is_navigational": true
  }
}
```

### Response

[Simulated Response](/simulate/property/create_property_json)

#### Status

```http hljs
201
```

#### Headers

```http hljs
API-Usage-Limit: 1/500
Content-Type: application/json; charset=utf-8
```

#### Body

```application/json; charset=utf-8 hljs
{
  "id": 35187304,
  "position": 13,
  "is_hidden": false,
  "is_navigational": true,
  "backoffice": true,
  "permalink": "country",
  "title": "Country"
}
```

## Get property

### Endpoint

```
GET /admin/properties/:property_id.json
```

### Request

#### Route

```
GET /admin/properties/1.json
```

#### Headers

```http hljs
Authorization: Basic ZGlnaXRhbC1nb29kczpjNTFjOTA3MDdhMTNjZTNmZmYyMTNhZmJiNWNkMTI3MA==
```

[Simulated Response](/simulate/property/get_property_json)

#### Status

```http hljs
200
```

#### Headers

```http hljs
API-Usage-Limit: 1/500
Content-Type: application/json; charset=utf-8
```

#### Body

```application/json; charset=utf-8 hljs
{
  "id": 1,
  "position": 8,
  "is_hidden": false,
  "is_navigational": true,
  "backoffice": false,
  "permalink": "producer",
  "title": "Producer"
}
```

# RecurringApplicationCharge

## Create recurring\_application\_charge

Application can have only one recurring charge at any given time.

### Endpoint

```
POST /admin/recurring_application_charge.json
```

### Parameters

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| recurring\_application\_charge\[monthly\]<br> required | amount of monthly payment |
| recurring\_application\_charge\[trial\_expired\_at\] | trial period ending date, by default it uses trial period from application |

### Request

#### Route

```
POST /admin/recurring_application_charge.json
```

#### Headers

```http hljs
Content-Type: application/json
Authorization: Basic ZGlnaXRhbC1nb29kczpjNTFjOTA3MDdhMTNjZTNmZmYyMTNhZmJiNWNkMTI3MA==
```

#### Body

```application/json hljs
{
  "recurring_application_charge": {
    "monthly": 200,
    "trial_expired_at": "2017-02-03"
  }
}
```

### Response

[Simulated Response](/simulate/recurringapplicationcharge/create_recurring_application_charge_json)

#### Status

```http hljs
201
```

#### Headers

```http hljs
API-Usage-Limit: 1/500
Content-Type: application/json; charset=utf-8
```

#### Body

```application/json; charset=utf-8 hljs
{
  "monthly": "200.0",
  "trial_expired_at": "2017-02-03",
  "created_at": "2024-11-13T00:56:44.379+03:00",
  "updated_at": "2024-11-13T00:56:44.379+03:00",
  "paid_till": "2017-02-03",
  "blocked": false
}
```

## add free days to recurring\_application\_charge

### Endpoint

```
PATCH /admin/recurring_application_charge/add_free_days.json
```

### Parameters

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| recurring\_application\_charge\[days\_count\] | how many free days you want to add, it is possible that paid\_till attribute would change but trial\_expired\_at would not, it is normal |

### Request

#### Route

```
PATCH /admin/recurring_application_charge/add_free_days.json
```

#### Headers

```http hljs
Content-Type: application/json
Authorization: Basic ZGlnaXRhbC1nb29kczpjNTFjOTA3MDdhMTNjZTNmZmYyMTNhZmJiNWNkMTI3MA==
```

#### Body

```application/json hljs
{
  "recurring_application_charge": {
    "days_count": 21
  }
}
```

### Response

[Simulated Response](/simulate/recurringapplicationcharge/add_free_days_to_recurring_application_charge_json)

#### Status

```http hljs
200
```

#### Headers

```http hljs
API-Usage-Limit: 1/500
Content-Type: application/json; charset=utf-8
```

#### Body

```application/json; charset=utf-8 hljs
{
  "monthly": "400.0",
  "trial_expired_at": "2024-12-12",

  "blocked": false
```

# Redirect

## Create redirect

### Endpoint

```
POST /admin/redirects.json
```

### Parameters

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| redirect\[old\_url\]<br> required | old url |
| redirect\[new\_url\]<br> required | new url |

### Request

#### Route

```
POST /admin/redirects.json
```

#### Headers

```http hljs
Content-Type: application/json
Authorization: Basic ZGlnaXRhbC1nb29kczpjNTFjOTA3MDdhMTNjZTNmZmYyMTNhZmJiNWNkMTI3MA==
```

#### Body

```application/json hljs
{
  "redirect": {
    "old_url": "/old_url",
    "new_url": "/new_url"
  }
}
```

### Response

[Simulated Response](/simulate/redirect/create_redirect_json)

#### Status

```http hljs
201
```

#### Headers

```http hljs
API-Usage-Limit: 1/500
Content-Type: application/json; charset=utf-8
```

#### Body

```application/json; charset=utf-8 hljs
{
  "id": 8,
  "old_url": "/old_url",
  "new_url": "/new_url",
  "created_at": "2024-11-13T00:57:53.319+03:00"
}
```

## Create redirect with removing redirect chains

### Endpoint

```
POST /admin/redirects.json
```

### Parameters

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| redirect\[old\_url\]<br> required | old url |
| redirect\[new\_url\]<br> required | new url |
| redirect\[remove\_redirect\_chains\] | if set to 1 and given a redirect A=>B when creating a new redirect B=>C, it will destroy old redirect (A=>B) and create new one (A=>C) |

### Request

#### Route

```
POST /admin/redirects.json
```

#### Headers

```http hljs
Content-Type: application/json
Authorization: Basic ZGlnaXRhbC1nb29kczpjNTFjOTA3MDdhMTNjZTNmZmYyMTNhZmJiNWNkMTI3MA==
```

#### Body

```application/json hljs
{
  "redirect": {
    "old_url": "/like_new_url",
    "new_url": "/so_new_url",
    "remove_redirect_chains": 1
  }
}
```

### Response

[Simulated Response](/simulate/redirect/create_redirect_with_removing_redirect_chains_json)

#### Status

```http hljs
201
```

#### Headers

```http hljs
API-Usage-Limit: 1/500
Content-Type: application/json; charset=utf-8
```

#### Body

```application/json; charset=utf-8 hljs
{
  "id": 12,
  "old_url": "/like_new_url",
  "new_url": "/so_new_url",
  "created_at": "2024-11-13T00:57:53.510+03:00"
}
```

# Review

## Create review

### Endpoint

```
POST /admin/reviews.json
```

### Parameters

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| review\[product\_id\]<br> required | product id |
| review\[author\]<br> required | author |
| review\[content\] | content |
| review\[email\] | email |
| review\[published\] | should be published? |
| review\[rating\] | product rating (1-10) |

### Request

#### Route

```
POST /admin/reviews.json
```

#### Headers

```http hljs
Content-Type: application/json
Authorization: Basic ZGlnaXRhbC1nb29kczpjNTFjOTA3MDdhMTNjZTNmZmYyMTNhZmJiNWNkMTI3MA==
```

#### Body

```application/json hljs
{
  "review": {
    "product_id": 1,
    "author": "Bob",
    "content": "Nice product! I'd like to buy it!",
    "email": "bob@gmail.com",
    "published": true,
    "rating": 7
  }
}
```

### Response

## Update review

### Endpoint

```
PUT /admin/reviews/:review_id.json
```

### Parameters

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| review\[content\] | content |

### Request

#### Route

```
PUT /admin/reviews/1.json
```

#### Headers

```http hljs
Content-Type: application/json
Authorization: Basic ZGlnaXRhbC1nb29kczpjNTFjOTA3MDdhMTNjZTNmZmYyMTNhZmJiNWNkMTI3MA==
```

#### Body

```application/json hljs
{
  "review": {
    "content": "Sweet product!"
  }
}
```

### Response

[Simulated Response](/simulate/review/update_review_json)

#### Status

```http hljs
200
```

#### Headers

```http hljs
API-Usage-Limit: 1/500
Content-Type: application/json; charset=utf-8
```

#### Body

```application/json; charset=utf-8 hljs
{
  "content": "Sweet product!",
```

# SalesChannel

## Create sales channel

### Endpoint

```
POST /admin/sales_channels.json
```

### Parameters

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| sales\_channel\[title\]<br> required | sales channel title |

### Request

#### Route

```
POST /admin/sales_channels.json
```

#### Headers

```http hljs
Content-Type: application/json
Authorization: Basic ZGlnaXRhbC1nb29kczpjNTFjOTA3MDdhMTNjZTNmZmYyMTNhZmJiNWNkMTI3MA==
```

#### Body

```application/json hljs
{
  "sales_channel": {
    "title": "sales channel title"
  }
}
```

### Response

[Simulated Response](/simulate/saleschannel/create_sales_channel_json)

#### Status

```http hljs
201
```

#### Headers

```http hljs
API-Usage-Limit: 1/500
Content-Type: application/json; charset=utf-8
```

#### Body

```application/json; charset=utf-8 hljs
{
  "id": 10,
  "title": "sales channel title",
  "state": null,
  "messages": [\
\
  ],
  "account_id": 1,
  "goods_setting_type": null,
  "goods_setting_id": null,
  "created_at": "2024-11-13T00:57:32.582+03:00",
  "updated_at": "2024-11-13T00:57:32.582+03:00",
  "application_id": 1,
  "last_rating_import_started_at": null,
  "last_feedbacks_import_started_at": null
}
```

```application/json; charset=utf-8 hljs
}
```

# Similar

| --- | --- |
| similar\_ids<br> required | similar ids array |

### Request

#### Route

```

```

```http hljs
Content-Type: application/json

```

#### Body

```application/json hljs
{
  "similar_ids": [\
    2\
  ]
}
```

### Response

[Simulated Response](/simulate/similar/create_similar_json)


```http hljs

Content-Type: application/json; charset=utf-8
```

```application/json; charset=utf-8 hljs
  "status": "ok"
}
```

# Stock Currency

## Create stock\_currency

Maximal quantity of currencies per account is 5.

### Endpoint

```
POST /admin/stock_currencies.json
```

### Parameters

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| stock\_currency\[code\]<br> required | Available codes:LVL, BYN, USD, EUR, EEK, LTL, AMD, KGS, MDL, EGP, CAD, JPY, TNB, TRY, AZN, PLN, ILS, CNY, BGN, GBP, RUR, UAH, AUD, GEL, AED, CHF, KZT, UZS, TJS, VND, TMT, MXN |
| stock\_currency\[is\_default\] | false by default, set it true to make this currency default for account |
| stock\_currency\[exchange\_rate\_use\_cb\] | true by default, set it false to use manual exchange rate |
| stock\_currency\[exchange\_rate\_manual\] | manual exchange rate |
| stock\_currency\[exchange\_rate\_percent\] | 0 by default, deviation as a percentage from defined exchange rate |

### Request

#### Route

```
POST /admin/stock_currencies.json
```

#### Headers

```http hljs
Content-Type: application/json
Authorization: Basic ZGlnaXRhbC1nb29kczpjNTFjOTA3MDdhMTNjZTNmZmYyMTNhZmJiNWNkMTI3MA==
```

#### Body

```application/json hljs
{
  "stock_currency": {
    "code": "KZT",
    "exchange_rate_percent": 10
  }
}
```

### Response

[Simulated Response](/simulate/stock_currency/create_stock_currency_json)

#### Status

```http hljs
201
```

#### Headers

```http hljs
API-Usage-Limit: 1/500
Content-Type: application/json; charset=utf-8
```

#### Body

```application/json; charset=utf-8 hljs
{
  "id": 93,
  "is_default": false,
  "exchange_rate_use_cb": true,
  "exchange_rate_manual": null,
  "exchange_rate_percent": "10.0",
  "exchange_rate_round": true,
  "code": "KZT",
  "title": "Казахский тенге",
  "cb_rate": "0.21",
  "unit": "тг.",
  "exchange_rate": "0.231"
}
```

# UserTask

```
POST /admin/user_tasks.json
```

### Parameters

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| user\_task\[title\]<br> required | user task title |
| user\_task\[description\]<br> required | user task description |
| user\_task\[assignee\_id\]<br> required | user id |
| user\_task\[deadline\_at\] | deadline |
| user\_task\[complete\] | is task completed? |
| user\_task\[order\_id\] | order id |

### Request

#### Route

```
POST /admin/user_tasks.json
```

#### Headers


```application/json hljs
    "description": "You should dispatch the order N2",

  }
```

# VariantField

## Create variant\_field

### Endpoint

```
POST /admin/variant_fields.json
```

### Parameters

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| variant\_field\[title\]<br> required | title |
| variant\_field\[handle\]<br> required | handle used in liquid |
| variant\_field\[type\]<br> required | VariantField::TextArea - textarea, VariantField::TextField - textfield |
| variant\_field\[position\] | position in variant\_fields list |
| variant\_field\[is\_hidden\] | boolean |

### Request

#### Route

```
POST /admin/variant_fields.json
```

#### Headers

```http hljs
Content-Type: application/json
Authorization: Basic ZGlnaXRhbC1nb29kczpjNTFjOTA3MDdhMTNjZTNmZmYyMTNhZmJiNWNkMTI3MA==
```

#### Body

```application/json hljs
{
  "variant_field": {
    "title": "Size",
    "handle": "size",
    "type": "VariantField::TextArea"
  }
}
```

### Response

[Simulated Response](/simulate/variantfield/create_variant_field_json)

#### Status

```http hljs
201
```

#### Headers

```http hljs
API-Usage-Limit: 1/500
Content-Type: application/json; charset=utf-8
```

#### Body

```application/json; charset=utf-8 hljs
{
  "id": 5,
  "application_id": 1,
  "type": "VariantField::TextArea",
  "handle": "size",
  "position": 3,
  "is_hidden": null,
  "title": "Size",
  "application_title": "Цифровые товары"
}
```

# Warehouse

```

```

### Parameters

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| warehouse\[title\]<br> required | warehouse title |
| warehouse\[position\] | warehouse position (1 - main priority) |

### Request

#### Route

```
POST /admin/warehouses.json
```

#### Headers

```http hljs
Content-Type: application/json
Authorization: Basic ZGlnaXRhbC1nb29kczpjNTFjOTA3MDdhMTNjZTNmZmYyMTNhZmJiNWNkMTI3MA==
```

#### Body

# Webhook

## Create webhook

### Endpoint

```
POST /admin/webhooks.json
```

### Parameters

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| webhook\[address\]<br> required | address |
| webhook\[topic\]<br> required | Topics: 'orders/create',<br> 'orders/update', 'orders/destroy',<br> 'products/create', 'products/update', 'client/create', 'client/update' |
| webhook\[format\_type\] | format of data sent by webhook: 'json' or 'xml' |
| webhook\[warehouse\_id\] | For 'orders/create', 'orders/update', 'orders/destroy' topics only, filters sent orders by warehouse |
| webhook\[sales\_channel\_id\] | For 'products/update' topic only, filters sent products by sales channel |
| webhook\[batch\_size\] | For 'products/create', 'products/update' topics only, products are sent in batches, default value: 10 |

### Request

#### Route

```
POST /admin/webhooks.json
```

#### Headers

```http hljs
Content-Type: application/json
Authorization: Basic ZGlnaXRhbC1nb29kczpjNTFjOTA3MDdhMTNjZTNmZmYyMTNhZmJiNWNkMTI3MA==
```

#### Body

```application/json hljs
{
  "webhook": {
    "address": "http://application.com/orders/create",
    "topic": "orders/create",
    "format_type": "json"
  }
}
```

### Response

[Simulated Response](/simulate/webhook/create_webhook_json)

#### Status

```http hljs
201
```

#### Headers

```http hljs
API-Usage-Limit: 1/500
Content-Type: application/json; charset=utf-8
```

#### Body

```application/json; charset=utf-8 hljs
{
  "id": 13,
  "address": "http://application.com/orders/create",
  "topic": "orders/create",
  "created_at": "2024-11-13T00:56:45.750+03:00",
  "format_type": "json",
  "warehouse_id": null,
  "sales_channel_id": null,
  "batch_size": null
}
```

## Update webhook

### Endpoint

```
PUT /admin/webhooks/:webhook_id.json
```

### Parameters

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| webhook\[address\] | address |
| webhook\[topic\] | Topics: 'orders/create',<br> 'orders/update', 'orders/destroy',<br> 'products/create', 'products/update', 'client/create', 'client/update' |
| webhook\[format\_type\] | format of data sent by webhook: json or xml |
| webhook\[warehouse\_id\] | For 'orders/create', 'orders/update', 'orders/destroy' topics only, filters sent orders by warehouse |
| webhook\[sales\_channel\_id\] | For 'products/update' topic only, filters sent products by sales channel |
| webhook\[batch\_size\] | For 'products/create', 'products/update' topics only, products are sent in batches, default value: 10 |

### Request

#### Route

```
PUT /admin/webhooks/15.json
```

#### Headers

```http hljs
Content-Type: application/json
Authorization: Basic ZGlnaXRhbC1nb29kczpjNTFjOTA3MDdhMTNjZTNmZmYyMTNhZmJiNWNkMTI3MA==
```

```application/json hljs

  "webhook": {
```
